***надзиратель.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надзиратель.html>надзира́тель</a> (6920)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надзиратель.html>надзира́тель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadzirátelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надзиратель.html>надзира́теля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надзиратель.html>надзира́тели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надзиратель.html>надзира́телей</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">надзира́тельница</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>warden, turnkey, supervisor, overseer</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надзор.html>надзо́р</a> (9976)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надзирать.html>надзира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadzirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="None mention" lang="ru">-∅</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-∅</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надзор.html>надзо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadzór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надзор.html>надзо́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надзор.html>надзо́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надзор.html>надзо́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>supervision</li>
<li>surveillance</li>
<li>inspectorate</li></ol>

***надлежать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надлежать.html>надлежа́ть</a> (6667)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Since the late 17th century. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">над-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nad-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежать.html>лежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ležátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly a calque of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">obliegen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надлежать.html>надлежа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadležátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> formal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have to <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to do as a requirement</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***надлежащий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надлежать.html>надлежа́щий</a> (13062)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надлежать.html>надлежа́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadležáščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надлежать.html>надлежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadležátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надлежать.html>надлежа́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadležáščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>proper, fitting, suitable

***надменный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надменный.html>надме́нный</a> (12250)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">надъменъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadŭmenŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">inflated, blown up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nadъmenъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">inflated, blown up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> - passive past participle of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nadǫti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">inflate, blow up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***надо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> (91)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">надъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nado</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nadъ</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nádo</span>) (+ instrumental case)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">variant of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nad</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> before words beginning with certain awkward consonant clusters such as <b>мн-</b></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> above, over
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мной</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nádo</b> mnoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>above</b> me</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nado</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">надобѣ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadobě</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from dative/locative singular of <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">надоба</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadoba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nadoba</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*na-</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*doba</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nádo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>(one) must, (it is) necessary</li>
<li>one needs, one wants, one has to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:уйти.html>уйти́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne <b>nádo</b> ujtí.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I <b>have to</b> leave.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>Так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tak jemú i <b>nádo</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He deserves it!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nádo</b> by</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(one) ought to</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The word combination, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a>, is used in combination with imperfective infinitive verbs. For example,
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a></b> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:печалиться.html>печа́литься</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne <b>nádo</b> <b>pečálitʹsja</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There is no need to be sad.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a></b> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ответ.html>отве́т</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne <b>nádo</b> <b>deržátʹ</b> otvét.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There is no need to answer.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пугать.html>пуга́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:белок.html>бе́лок</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne <b>nádo</b> býlo <b>pugátʹ</b> bélok.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There was no need to scare the squirrels.</span></div></dd></dl>

***надоедать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надоедать.html>надоеда́ть</a> (13507)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">надое́д-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadojéd-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надоедать.html>надоеда́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadojedátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надоесть.html>надое́сть</a></b>)

<ol><li>to bore</li>
<li>to bother, to pester, to molest, to worry, to annoy, to plague</li></ol>

***надоесть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надоесть.html>надое́сть</a> (2018)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">приеда́ться</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prijedátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надоесть.html>надое́сть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadojéstʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надоедать.html>надоеда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bore
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ей</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:надоесть.html>надое́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jej <b>nadojélo</b> čitátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">she is tired of reading</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to bother, to pester, to molest, to worry, to annoy, to plague
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>сме́рти</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:надоесть.html>надое́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on mne do smérti <b>nadojél</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'm bored to death with him</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***надорвать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надорвать.html>надорва́ть</a> (19243)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">надо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nado-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надорвать.html>надорва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadorvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надрывать.html>надрыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tear slightly</li>
<li>to overstrain, to overtax, to undermine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надорвать.html>надорва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadorvátʹ</b> svoí síly</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to overtax one's strength; knock oneself out</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надорвать.html>надорва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лос</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadorvátʹ</b> sebé gólos</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to overstrain one's voice</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надорвать.html>надорва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душу</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadorvátʹ</b> dušu komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rend smb's heart; harrow smb's soul</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надорвать.html>надорва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:животик.html>живо́тики</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadorvátʹ</b> živótiki</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> to split one's sides with laughter</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***надорваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надорваться.html>надорва́ться</a> (23482)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надорвать.html>надорва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadorvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надорваться.html>надорва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadorvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надрываться.html>надрыва́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tear slightly</li>
<li>to overstrain oneself, to exert oneself to the utmost, to knock oneself out, to bust a gut</li>
<li>to shout, to cry, to cry at the top of one's lungs</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надорвать.html>надорва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadorvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***надписать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надписать.html>надписа́ть</a> (28285)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">над-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nad-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надписать.html>надписа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadpisátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">надпи́сывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to label, to caption, to write an inscription on</li>
<li>to write <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">something that is above something else, e.g. a missing letter above the line</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надпись.html>на́дпись</a> (1930)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надписать.html>надписа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadpisátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to caption, to write an inscription on</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with typical stress shift (compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подпись.html>по́дпись</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pódpisʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запись.html>за́пись</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zápisʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, etc.).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надпись.html>на́дпись</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nádpisʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надпись.html>на́дписи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надпись.html>на́дписи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надпись.html>на́дписей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>inscription, writing</li>
<li>dedication <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">on a book</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>address <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">on an envelope</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>legend <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">on a coin, medal, map</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надрывать.html>надрыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
